Ambassador Yan Huiqing Returns to the Country Yesterday and Arrives in Shanghai 131

Will enter Beijing today or tomorrow to pay respects to the authorities

Then go to Tianjin to handle personal matters Our Ambassador to Russia, Mr. Yan Huiqing, arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon at about 5:00 pm aboard the Italian postal ship Conte Rosso. He is scheduled to enter Beijing today or tomorrow to pay respects to Chairman Lin and President Wang. He plans to stay in Beijing for one or two days, then return to Tianjin to rest and handle personal matters. Afterwards, he will come to Beijing again to report everything to the Central Government, request instructions on foreign policy, and then return to his post in six months. The details are recorded as follows:

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday, Will Go to Beijing Today or Tomorrow 132

Ambassador Yan arrived in Shanghai at about 4:50 pm yesterday afternoon aboard the Italian postal ship Conte Rosso, which docked at the Qichang Wharf in Pudong. After disembarking, Ambassador Yan immediately transferred to the Jianghai Customs Jinghui small ferry to cross the river. At about 5:30 pm, he landed at the Bund Copper Man Wharf on Nanjing Road and went directly to the Cathay Hotel to rest. Ambassador Yan will take a train to Beijing today or tomorrow to pay respects to Chairman Lin and President Wang, and then return to Tianjin. During Ambassador Yan's return to the country, all embassy duties will be temporarily handled by Counselor Wu Nanru.

Wang and Song Both Send Representatives to Welcome 133

Those who went to the wharf yesterday to welcome Ambassador Yan included Shen Jinding, representing Executive Yuan President and Minister of Foreign Affairs Wang Jingwei; Yang Guangshao, representing National Economic Council Standing Committee Member Song Ziwen; Geng Jiaji, representing Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng; Zhou Jue, Secretary of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; Yu Ming, Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; Zhao Tiezhang, Section Chief; Zhang Ming, former Special Envoy to Nepal; Yan Fuqing and Yan Deqing, younger brothers of Ambassador Yan; Soviet Consul General in Shanghai Spirivinnek; and more than fifty friends and relatives of Ambassador Yan and reporters from various newspapers. The representatives of Wang and Song took the Jinghui small ferry to cross the river, the representative of Mayor Wu took the Public Security small ferry to cross the river, and the relatives of Ambassador Yan took the Haigang Quarantine Station's Yue Fei and Huatuo small ferries to cross the river. The Public Concession Water Police Department specially sent six Chinese and Western detectives yesterday to accompany the Jinghui small ferry to cross the river for protection.

Mr. Yan Looks Older Than Before 134

Mr. Yan was appointed as envoy to the United States after the September 18th Incident in 1931. Soon after, he represented the National Government as a plenipotentiary representative to the League of Nations, and was transferred to be the Ambassador to Russia. It has been two years since he returned to the country yesterday. Although he has experienced wind and fatigue, his spirit is as always, but the number of his white hair has increased more than before. When Mr. Yan arrived in Shanghai yesterday, he was wearing a tweed suit, a blue wool overcoat, and a gray wool hat. His attitude was natural and his conversation was quite refreshing. He is truly a rare talent in our country.

Mr. Yan Meets Reporters in the Ship 135

Ambassador Yan met with reporters from various newspapers in the ship. According to him, he departed from Moscow on December 8th last year and boarded a ship from Italy on January 10th. This time he returned to the country without any mission. He just requested leave from the Central Government to return to the country and report on the situation abroad because he had not returned to the country for a long time. He has been away from the country for two years, and is not familiar with the domestic situation. He is eager to return to the country, but he has been unable to do so due to busy affairs. Now that he has safely returned to the country, unless there is an emergency, he plans to stay for several months and then return to his post to cancel the leave.

Ambassador Yan Huiqing Photographed on Landing (Gong Shuxian) 136

Will Enter Beijing Today or Tomorrow and Go to Tianjin Immediately 137

Ambassador Yan continued, "I am scheduled to enter Beijing the day after tomorrow (i.e., today or tomorrow) to pay respects to the Acting Foreign Minister Wang and report on the situation abroad over the past two years. I will decide to stay in Beijing for one day and then cross the river to change trains to Tianjin for a short stay. Then I will return to the capital to discuss all issues with the Central Government. Of course, diplomatic issues will also be discussed. During my return to the country, I will pay attention to observing the feelings of the people, because national affairs should be based on public opinion. The government acts according to public opinion, and the overseas envoys only follow the orders of the government, in other words, listen to public opinion. For two years, I have been separated from the national situation and public opinion. Telegrams and newspapers cannot fully explain everything, so it is best to observe in person. Therefore, the purpose of this trip back to the country is purely to observe public opinion, and according to the regulations of various countries, all overseas officials must return to the country once a year to observe public opinion and understand the national situation. I have been abroad for more than two years, and this return to the country is also expected."

Russo-Japanese War is Quite Possible 138

"The relationship between Japan and Russia has become increasingly tense recently, and the outbreak of war is quite possible. However, the remarks I made that were transmitted by the Hong Kong telegram are somewhat exaggerated. The Soviet Union is paying close attention to the Far East. On the one hand, it hopes that peace can be maintained, and on the other hand, it prepares to give a head-on blow to the aggressors. As for our country, we hope to maintain peace in East Asia, but we also need to strengthen our national strength to deal with the current emergency."

Russia Will Never Recognize the Puppet Organization 139

"After the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, the Soviet Union has a very good feeling towards China. The results of the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan are very good. The second Five-Year Plan is currently being implemented. The Soviet Union will never recognize the Manchukuo puppet state. However, because of the geographical location, actual exchanges are inevitable. Regarding the negotiations on the Chinese Eastern Railway, the Soviet Union hopes to obtain considerable compensation before it can be transferred. The resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia is a powerful guarantee for peace in the Far East."

European Countries are Preparing for War More and More Urgently 140

"In the past, all countries that recognized the League of Nations relied on the League of Nations as a guarantee to maintain world peace. However, since the Sino-Japanese Incident, European countries have felt that the power of the League of Nations is not enough to maintain world peace and feel the need for self-defense, which has led to the trend of countries preparing for war. European countries are paying close attention to the Far East, because they all firmly believe that the Far East Incident is sufficient to affect European countries."

Regret the Decline of the League of Nations' Prestige 141

Regarding the situation of the League of Nations in Geneva, according to Mr. Yan, he left Geneva at the end of February last year, and it has been a year since then. The General Assembly of the League of Nations was held on January 15th, and our representative was Minister Gu Gong. He expressed regret over the decline of the League of Nations' prestige, because the decline of the League of Nations' prestige is sufficient to make international suspicions arise, and each seeks a way to deal with it, so conflicts are easy to occur. The League of Nations is a shared League of Nations of all countries, not unique to China, and the rights and obligations of all countries in the League of Nations are better than China's. If the League of Nations declares bankruptcy, the impact on all countries will also be greater than on China."

Most Countries' Economies are Declining 142

When asked by reporters about his observations during his travels in Europe in the past two years, he replied that he had been in Europe for more than two years and traveled among various countries. He felt that the current situation in Europe was very different from before. The most obvious was the decline of the economies of various countries, year after year, and its impact on the future would naturally be great. The increase in the number of unemployed people in various countries is a great crisis, which is what he has gained from his travels in Europe.

As for the trade agreement that the former Chairman of Xinjiang Province, Jin Shuren, had signed with the Soviet Union without authorization, it has been investigated and confirmed by former Minister Luo. Yuntaishan Cave Collapsed Due to Snow Pressure 145

Traffic on the eastern section of the Longhai Railway is interrupted. The Longhai Railway Water and Land Joint Transportation Office of this port received an urgent telegram from Laoyao yesterday, which stated that heavy snow had fallen in Haizhou for several days and accumulated heavily. The Yuntaishan Xikou Cave suddenly collapsed on the 2nd, and the cave was submerged, interrupting traffic. How the Railway Bureau will handle it has not yet been clearly stated. As for whether there were any casualties when the cave collapsed, it was not mentioned in the telegram because it was brief. However, the tracks in the cave were crushed by the rocks, and the loss must be considerable. It may not be possible to reopen and repair it in a short period of time. The reporter has investigated the situation and recorded it as follows:

Heavy Snow in Haizhou 146

The newly opened port of Laoyao in Haizhou was opened to navigation in November last year. There are often extreme storms in the Yingyoumen channel. The wave-stopping embankment project built by the Dutch Port Authority is in active progress, and the entire project will not be completed until the autumn of this year. At that time, the impact of the waves can be reduced. From the first day of this month, the weather in Laoyao and Xinpu was extremely cold, and heavy snow fell until yesterday morning. The snow accumulated thickly everywhere, causing the water and land construction work to be stopped.

The Cave Collapsed 147

Yuntaishan in Laoyao is all hard stone. The Dutch Port Authority has opened a large mountain cave of one or two hundred meters in the Chenjiagang section, and the Longhai Railway has laid railway tracks to connect the train to Laoyao, connecting water and land joint transportation. At the same time, the Dutch company also excavated mountain stones and filled a long wave-stopping embankment. From the first day, the heavy snow did not stop day and night, and accumulated very deeply. The Xikou Cave of Yuntaishan collapsed suddenly on the afternoon of the second day due to the high pressure of heavy snow. The mountain collapsed and the ground collapsed, and the sound shook far and wide, and the tracks were also submerged.

Traffic Interrupted 148

Laoyao New Port Joint Transportation is currently in the process of transporting large quantities of goods. Grains and other items from the northwest rely entirely on train transportation. Now that the newly opened cave in Yuntaishan has collapsed suddenly, the railway traffic to Laoyao has been interrupted. The Longhai Railway's trains cannot pass through Yuntaishan. Transportation is interrupted. The Railway Bureau has not yet had a definite solution after receiving the report.

Number of Chinese Directors in the Public Works Department 150

Taxpayer Association Executive Committee

Resolved to negotiate for an increase

To make it equal to the proportion of taxes. Guowen News Agency said that the Shanghai Concession Taxpayer Association held its fifth executive committee meeting at 5:00 pm yesterday. Those present were Cheng Xiechun, Xu Jiqing, Xu Wenzhao, Chu Huiseng, Sun Qiuping, Shi Zhikun, Wang Xiaolai, Cao Zhigong, Yu Zhongxian, Yu Hualong, Zhang Yichen, Chen Binghui, Jin Zongcheng, Shen Tianxin, Gu Wensheng, Cai Qiajun, and Ma Junshuo. Regarding the number of Chinese directors in the Public Works Department of the Public Concession being five, it was originally a temporary measure. Moreover, the proportion of taxes paid by Chinese people was 55% in the past, and that of foreigners was 45%. According to the Public Works Department's investigation recently, the proportion of taxes paid by Chinese people has increased to 64%, and that of foreigners only accounts for 36%. Since the amount of taxes paid by Chinese people has increased, the number of Chinese directors should also be increased in proportion to this, so as not to lose the fairness of the matter. It was resolved to actively negotiate for the number of Chinese directors in the Public Works Department of the Public Concession to be increased to be equal to the proportion of taxes paid. Other proposals were also discussed, and the meeting adjourned at 6:30 pm.

Two China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Ships Encounter Danger 151

Liji and Gongping Run Aground and Damaged

Liji Runs Aground The Liji, a shallow-water ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which travels between Hankou and Changsha, was carrying goods to Hunan this time. When it was about to reach Xindi, the ship ran aground due to the exceptionally shallow river water. Because the ship was heavily loaded, it ran aground and could not be towed. It immediately sent an urgent telegram to Hankou to send the Liyuan to fly to the area, first loading the goods on the ship, and then towing it. According to the telegram, the Hunan waterway was also suddenly blocked, and even shallow-water ships could not pass. However, the Kuaili has arrived in Nanjing and can come to Shanghai today. The Changxing, a Sanbei ship, is still stranded in Madang and has not been towed out. Now it can only wait for the water to rise.

Gongping Engine Damage The Gongping of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is the largest of all the ships. This time, it was transporting goods from Shanghai to Qingdao. At 2:00 pm on the 1st, it sailed out of Shanghai. On the afternoon of the 2nd, when the ship was in the middle of its journey, the ship's shaft suddenly broke and a part of the engine blades was damaged. It also encountered strong winds at sea, which was very dangerous. Yesterday morning, the shipowner sent an urgent telegram to Shanghai, reporting the broken shaft and damaged blades, making it difficult to navigate and fearing accidents. After receiving the report, the bureau immediately replied with a wireless telegram, ordering the shipowner to quickly turn around and return to Shanghai, because a part of the ship's engine blades had not been completely destroyed and could be used, so it ordered it to return to Shanghai and not go to Qingdao. It then received another telegram stating that the Gongping was already on its way back and would arrive in port today. After it arrives in Shanghai and is inspected, it will be sent to the dock for major repairs.

Two Roads Reduce Grain Transportation Costs 153

The Two Roads Administration received a telegram from the former Fengtian Railway Department (The Ministry, in order to relieve rural areas and regulate food supply, has specially instructed the said road to reduce grain transportation prices to the lowest possible limit, so as to provide relief and facilitate transportation), etc. Upon receipt, it was immediately forwarded to the Traffic Department to draft a plan, which was submitted by the bureau to the Ministry of Railways for approval. From February 1st, the two roads will transport grain and charge according to the fifth class, minus 15%, for a period of six months. The scope of the grain should be limited to barley, corn, miscellaneous grains (except as otherwise specified), sorghum, millet, glutinous millet (except as otherwise specified), glutinous millet, hulled millet, buckwheat, rice (except as otherwise specified), rye, wheat, and grain. However, it is found that the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway line transports wheat and rice (except as otherwise specified) from Wuxi to Shanghai North Station or Maigen Road. The original fixed price is one yuan and seven cents per ton for a whole car. Only 10% additional handling fee is required, and no 20% additional price is added. This special price will be temporarily suspended. If the special grain price is not continued after the six-month period expires, it can be restored.

Cargo Ship Sinks in Huangpu River Yesterday Afternoon 156

Ship Owner's Wife and Four Others Overturned

The bricks and stones on board were also submerged. Huadong News Agency reported that a cargo ship was going south on the Huangpu River yesterday noon when it suddenly capsized, killing four people. A reporter from Huadong News Agency heard the news and drove to investigate the details. The details are as follows:

Cause of the Capsizing At 12:45 yesterday noon, a cargo ship owned by ship owner Yang Huiwen was sailing south in the Huangpu River at Renji Road Pier. In addition to five men and two women on board, there were also 100,000 long rectangular bricks tied with sacks. Yesterday, there were strong winds and huge waves at the same time. A large steamer passed three or four feet away from the ship, and the waves crashed and hit the stern of the cargo ship, causing the stern to flood. In addition, the gale roared and blew the sails of the cargo ship sideways, so the stern sank first, and the entire ship capsized. Police Rescue After receiving the news, the water patrol police immediately drove a boat to rescue them. Three people were rescued, including ship boss Yang Huiwen, and crew members Song Ziyuan and Li Jinbiao. Two Westerners also bravely rescued three people in the water, including Wu Decai, Wang Zhaosheng, and the ship owner's wife, Yang Shi, but Yang Shi was dead when she was rescued. As for the goods that were picked up by the water patrol police, only a few bags of bricks and scattered wooden roots of sails were found.

Number of Deaths According to statistics after the incident, the total number of deaths was four, including Yang Shi (female), 26 years old, the wife of the ship's crew; Daxizi (male), 7 years old, the ship owner's son; Xiaomaotou (female), 3 years old, the ship owner's daughter; and Xiao Asan, 2 years old (male), also the ship owner's son. Except for Yang Shi, the remaining bodies have not been picked up. The cargo on the ship and personal property were all sunk in the Huangpu River. It is said that the bricks were transported by the Zhongshan Bridge Public Company, and their value was 360 yuan.

General National Currency Transformed into Ingots 163

= The Ministry of Finance Had Previously Issued Orders Prohibiting It =

= Unemployed Merchants Arrested for Illegally Melting =

Since our country implemented the abolition of taels and the conversion to yuan last year, the Ministry of Finance has formally issued an order for consistent compliance. All silver furnace agencies must close down and must not melt the general national currency into ingots. Although the general silver furnace operators have argued with reason and appealed to the authorities, the result was unsuccessful. Now, unemployed silver furnace merchants Qi Chufa, Mao Zhoufu, and others have recently opened a Ruitai sign at No. 20 Yixingli, Qipu Road, specializing in melting silver, and established a workshop at No. 41 Tiantong Road. This was discovered by the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and it was learned that these people violated the ministry's order and still melted the general national currency into ingots. Detective Hu Kui-sheng and Gu Lian-cheng were specially dispatched to report to the First Special District Court at around 7 p.m. the day before yesterday and signed a search warrant, which was issued to the Huisi Patrol Room in charge, and Western Inspector Bai Hua and detective Liang Yuliang were dispatched to jointly arrest five people from Shaoxing, Qian Guoxun, Zhou Huilin, Chen Jinshan, Shen Yushu, and Tong Dasheng, at No. 41 Tiantong Road, and then arrested Qi Chufa at No. 20 Yixingli, Qipu Road. However, Mao Zhoufu was not arrested. Eight hundred and seventy-nine double-corner ingots, twenty-six silver ingots, sixty-two pounds of broken silver, four iron models, two clay models, seven silver-plated gold bracelets, fifteen ear scoops, seven earrings, twenty-five rings, ten hairpins, fourteen account books, and thirteen stamps were also seized at the two locations and taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. According to police lawyer Jiang Baolian, the case was requested to be postponed in order to continue the investigation. Detective Gu Lian-cheng of the Municipal Public Security Bureau also stated that the case was a secret report from the superior, stating that there were places such as Qipu Road and Tiantong Road in the Public Concession that were melting the general currency into ingots, violating the central government's order, so the patrol room was joined to arrest them. Qian Guoxun confessed that he used to be in the silver furnace industry, and this time he was hired by Qi Chufa. His salary was seven corners a day. The ingots that were seized were not melted by us, but were shipped from Fujian. We specialize in melting old-fashioned silverware jewelry from various silver shops into ingots and selling them to silver shops to make new-style jewelry for sale. Because the silverware received is of different quality, it must be melted into ingots so that the quality is equal and there is no difference. Zhou Huilin and Tong Tiansheng also confessed that they were boarding there and did not know about the rest. Chen Jinshan confessed that he was hired by Qi Chufa and his daily salary was six corners. Shen Yushu confessed that he came to Shanghai on January 27 to help Qi. Qi Chufa confessed that he and Mao Zhoufu opened a Ruitai sign at Yixingli, Qipu Road, and started business on January 1 of this year. A total of about 1,000 ingots were melted and sold to Wensheng and Laofengxiang Silver Shops to manufacture jewelry. As for the ingots that were seized, they were shipped from Fujian. Because the various silver shops in Fujian Province melted all kinds of old-style silverware and gilded jewelry into ingots, but some of them were made of copper or gold and could not be extracted, so I asked my shop to use medicine to remelt them to extract gold and copper. Regarding the national currency, if there are any that cannot be used, they are also melted, etc. Finally, Jiang Yiping, Qi's agent lawyer, stated that the case was filed by the Municipal Public Security Bureau to request assistance from the patrol room, but I don't know what articles of law were cited to prosecute. The lawyer searched the criminal law and there were no explicit provisions for this kind of case, and all the people who were arrested were residents of the concession. According to the agreement, people who are innocent cannot be detained. It should be allowed to be released on bail pending further instructions. Judge Wu Tingqi reported and ordered Qi Chufa to pay a deposit of 3,000 yuan, Qian, Chen, and Shen to each pay a deposit of 500 yuan, and Zhou and Tong to each pay a deposit that can be summoned at any time to go out pending verification.

○ ○ ○ ○ The relevant parts. According to the criminal law, civil servants must strictly abide by the confidentiality of their duties, and the place of office does not dare to interfere with the law. I hope you will forgive me. Establishment of the British Preparatory College 164

British famous educator Mr. Kangpu was hired by the Shanghai Public Works Bureau in 1904 AD to be in charge of the affairs of Huatong Public School.

Great contribution. After Mr. Kang returned to China last spring after his term of office expired, he saw that there were many young people from other countries who went to study in the UK, but they were often troubled by the lack of considerable guidance. It was not easy to be admitted to universities such as Oxford and Cambridge. Therefore, he created a college in Lizimeng, eight miles away from London, the British capital, specifically for students to prepare for university entrance examinations. Lizimeng is located on the Thames River, which is famous for its beautiful scenery, and is very close to London's suburban parks. The location is quiet, the customs are simple, not as noisy and polluted as London's population, so it is very suitable for students to concentrate on their studies. Moreover, the living standards in the area are not as high as those in London, so the fees are very low. The monthly tuition and board is only 15 to 17 British pounds per person. Young people in our country who want to study in the UK should pay attention to it. As for the registration procedures and other details, you can contact Mr. Huang Zhuming of Huatong Public School, No. 63 Heske Road, Shanghai, to inquire and contact.

Li Minzhou's Funeral Today 169

=Police Authorizes Special Route Through Nanjing Road=

=New General Manager Elected, Nephew Succeeds= The incident of Xin Xin Company's General Manager Li Minzhou being shot and killed by Zhou Zhanyuan, the deputy head of patrol, after dismissing Zhou has been widely reported. It is now heard that Li Minzhou's funeral will be held at 2 PM today, with special permission from the police to turn from Xizang Road into Nanjing Road and circle the company. It is known that Li went to Australia to do business at a young age and, like Guo Shun, Guo Le, Ma Yingbiao, and others who are current general managers of the Sincere and Wing On companies, was a prominent overseas Chinese figure in Australia. He returned to China eight years ago when Xin Xin Company was founded and immediately joined the company as a supervisor. Four years ago, he was promoted to manager. Last year, after Liu Xiji passed away, Li succeeded him as general manager. He was known for his sharp determination and diligence in handling matters. The company experienced internal labor unrest four or five years ago, which Li resolved smoothly. In recent years, the business has flourished, returning to its former glory, all thanks to Li's efforts. Now, he has been assassinated, and all sectors of society are deeply saddened. It is now heard that the company's board of directors elected Li Ze yesterday to succeed as general manager. Li Ze is Minzhou's direct nephew, currently the deputy manager of the company. He previously spent many years in Hong Kong and Guangzhou engaged in banking and import-export trade. He is as astute and decisive as his uncle. Over the years, when Minzhou was away on business, Li Ze acted on his behalf, handling matters in an orderly manner and was highly valued by the directors. He is more than capable of carrying on Li's business. Deputy Manager and Treasurer Zheng Wenzhu will remain in his original position, and Tang Chengzhang has been promoted to deputy manager. Both have served department stores for many years and have extensive experience, so there will be no impact on the company's business prospects.

Land Value Tax for Industry Associations 175

The acreage should be sent separately for review.

The Finance Bureau replied to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to inform them that the Finance Bureau had responded to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce regarding the request of various industry associations to exempt land value tax for association premises. The reply stated, "Your Chamber's Public Letter No. 758 states that the industry associations, etc., request exemption from land value tax on the public property of the respective associations, and requests that it be examined and approved. Upon inquiry, the association's request was submitted to the Bureau, and it was decided that the request for exemption from land value tax should be made by the associations themselves, specifying the acreage and use of public property, and submitted to this Bureau for review and handling in conjunction with the Land Bureau. This has been instructed in the record. In response to the letter, please inform them accordingly."

Ministry of Industry Urges Commercial Federation to Promptly Recommend Labor and Management Representatives 176

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the 18th Labor Conference, decided by the 64th UN Council, will be held on May 14 this year in Geneva. In addition to receiving a notification from the International Labor Bureau to dispatch representatives and advisors, this year, due to the election of directors at the conference, and international competition, the government has already appointed Li Pingheng, Director of the Labor Department of the Ministry of Industry, as the government representative, and Xie Dongfa as an advisor. At the same time, Guo Shun, Chairman of the All-China Federation of Industry, and Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, have been notified to promptly determine the management representatives for easy dispatch. Xin Sheng News Agency reporters visited Qian Chengxu of the General Chamber of Industry yesterday to inquire about the selection of management representatives for this session, and the agenda of the conference, including the parts related to China. Qian replied that according to the written notice from the International Labor Bureau forwarded by the Ministry of Industry, the conference agenda includes seven items: (1) Reducing working hours, (2) Unemployment insurance and unemployment relief methods, (3) Rest and shift methods for glass factory workers. These three items were discussed at the 17th conference last year but were not concluded and were retained for discussion this year. As for the agenda for this session, it is (1) Preserving the original disability and death insurance rights of workers when they move from one country to another, (2) Revising the Occupational Disease Compensation Act in the convention, (3) Employing women as miners, (4) Revising the Women's Night Work Convention. The above seven items, because they are largely unrelated to the current labor and management situation and organization in China, the management side does not feel excited. Up to now, no representatives have been produced. However, an order from the Ministry was received yesterday urging action, so it cannot be delayed any longer. The matter will be discussed with the Federation of Chambers of Commerce in the next day or two. If there is a solution, people will be selected to fill the positions. As for the funding, the industrial and commercial sectors are feeling exhausted this year, which is far less easy to raise than in previous years. It is expected that the government will be requested to subsidize the funds.

Ministry of Transportation Collects Documents 177

Preparing to Negotiate the Tunan Case

Japanese Merchants Counterclaim 74,000 Yuan

The entire case has been transferred to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The China Merchants Bureau's Tunan ship was sunk by the Japanese ship Changchun Maru, resulting in heavy losses. Afterwards, the Japanese refused arbitration and filed a counterclaim. The Ministry of Transportation has instructed the Bureau to send all procedures to Beijing to prepare for negotiations with the Japanese side to pursue compensation. The situation is recorded as follows:

Japanese Side Files Counterclaim 178

Since the China Merchants Bureau presented to the Ministry of Transportation for approval to submit the case of the Changchun Maru sinking the Tunan ship for arbitration, a court of arbitration was formed in Shanghai, with each party hiring a notary to investigate. The China Merchants Bureau entrusted Guwo Lawyers as representatives to contact Dalian Steampship Company, but was severely rejected. Recently, the company attributed the sinking of the Tunan ship by the Changchun Maru to the Chinese ship. Therefore, they filed a counterclaim against the China Merchants Bureau, seeking compensation for various damages and repairs to the Changchun Maru, totaling more than 73,996 yuan, and specially sent a letter from the Dalian Steampship Company to the China Merchants Bureau to collect the money.

Ministry of Transportation Has Notified the Ministry of Foreign Affairs 179

On January 26, the China Merchants Bureau presented to the Ministry of Transportation, requesting the central government to promptly conduct serious negotiations with the Japanese side and order the Dalian Steampship Company to quickly compensate for all losses of the sunk Tunan ship to avoid prolonged suspension of the case. The Ministry of Transportation has reported the China Merchants Bureau and consulted the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to formally negotiate with the Japanese Embassy. The Bureau received instructions from the Ministry of Transportation yesterday, stating that the case of the Japanese ship Changchun Maru sinking the Tunan ship has been consulted with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to formally negotiate with the Japanese side.

Collect All Case Documents 180

The Ministry of Transportation also issued Order No. 1892 to the China Merchants Bureau, instructing it to collect all correspondence between the China Merchants Bureau, entrusting Guwo Lawyers, and the Japanese Dalian Steampship Company, as well as letters from the Japanese side requesting counterclaims, in the Tunan sinking case, and transfer them to Beijing for investigation during negotiations. Yesterday afternoon, the China Merchants Bureau complied and prepared fifteen copies of the documents related to the exchange between the two sides in the Tunan case, attached with a formal document, and submitted them to the Ministry of Transportation.

Red Swastika Society's Relief Measures for the Dongping Flood 181

Hou Sushuang's memorandum on dredging methods. The Shanghai General Office of the Southeast Main Branch of the Red Swastika Society, seeing that the flood victims in Dongping, Shandong, were still trapped, specially appealed to all sectors of Shanghai with the slogan "Save a life with five jiao," and remitted 2,000 yuan for relief, while President Xiong Xiling appealed to various charities for donations. It is heard that Hou Sushuang, president of the Jinan Red Swastika Society, sent another letter to Xiong Xiling yesterday, reporting the reasons why the floodwaters in Dongping have not receded, and proposing two relief measures, which are extremely pertinent. They are specially excerpted below to inform those who care about treating the Yellow River: (Respectfully, I just received your telegram, knowing that you have allocated one thousand yuan from your office to relieve the flood in Dongping, and then jointly with various charities, advertised for donations. I see that you deeply care about the suffering and are deeply concerned about the drowning. Under the cover of washing, I can't help but feel grateful. The water in Dongping this year was a little later than other counties, so the report to the provincial government was also later than other counties, but because it is located in a low-lying area, the water from various counties has gathered, flooding more than 4,000 hectares of fields, which are still more than a zhang deep. Therefore, the disaster areas in other places have mostly planted wheat, while Dongping is still a vast expanse of water. Even by next spring, there will be no hope of sowing. The water from the Qingyun and Yunhe rivers in Dongping has always entered the Yellow River through Qinghe Gate (the Daqing River is in the east of the city, the Yun River is in the west, and the Yellow River is in the north). This year, the Yellow River water flooded back too fiercely, and the river gate was silted up, causing it to stagnate and not flow. The area west of the city has suddenly become a wetland. Fortunately, the Qingyun and Yunhe rivers have not been in danger this year, otherwise the city would not be safe. There are nearly 200,000 flood victims. The relief funds released by various parties before amount to no more than two or three jiao per person. There are only two porridge factories, one set up by the Swastika Society in the city, and one set up by the Investigation and Release Office in Anshan Town, west of the city (15 li from the city). Now, Du Shaopeng of the Investigation and Release Office has also obtained permission to set up another one at the Daimiao (50 li west of the city). The cotton clothes distributed by various parties are in 5,000 sets, close to 6,000. This is the current relief situation. As for the water diversion methods, there are permanent and temporary ones. The permanent one is to dredge the Qingyun and Yunhe rivers, and build dikes to raise the water level, so that the Qingyun and Yunhe rivers flow to the Qinghe Gate to suppress the Yellow River, and then build a gate to control the opening and closing, so that the Yellow River will never back up. In this way, 4,000 hectares of disaster fields will be completely drained, and the areas that have accumulated water over the years will also become fertile. However, this cannot be achieved without 600,000 yuan. It is planned to appeal to various parties to gradually complete this major project. The temporary emergency relief is to excavate the Qinghe Gate, so that the current accumulated water can have a way out (Huihang recently went to the Dongping disaster area with Du Shaopeng, Zhou Baipeng, and others, so they made an equal appeal. Huihang also promised to submit a statement to the Ministry of Finance). I went to survey the siltation the other day. The highest is less than 20 li. If 2,000 to 3,000 strong men and refugees are gathered, it can be completed in one month. However, it is currently in the solid ice period. It can be started on the tenth day of the first lunar month, but earthwork requires no more than 20,000 yuan. There is already 11,000, 7,000 yuan from the Provincial Political Council, and 4,000 yuan from Qian Junren, which has not yet been allocated. If we add your donation, it will be 12,000 yuan, which is still 8,000 short. If this project is completed, 1,000 hectares of nearby fields can be drained and planted with late wheat (wheat can still be planted in February of the old calendar). This is what has been done successfully in the past few years. If 4,000 hectares can be fully harvested for half a season, it is necessary to purchase a mud-digging steamship to constantly shuttle back and forth for dredging. However, the price of this ship is quite high. The Shandong Construction Department has ordered two ships from the province's Luda Factory for dredging the Xiaozheng River, each costing 80,000 yuan (it was originally intended to borrow one from Qinghe Gate for use, but unfortunately, it could not be transported). I don't know if there are cheaper ones in the Shanghai factory. I also hope that you will take the time to inquire about it, so that we can consider purchasing it. The province government is likely to allocate these funds, but it will have to wait three months. This is the plan for this part. If the entire permanent plan is completed, the 4,000 hectares of fields will be permanently free from flooding, and two seasons can be harvested. Dongping's prosperity can be A-grade in western Shandong. Dongping City has many mountains on the east side, and the land is barren and the people are poor. The west side is purely fertile land, which has been troubled by the Qingyun and Yunhe rivers for decades. The rich have all moved and dispersed, and the common people make a living by fishing and shrimp, resulting in the name Dongping Lake. This year, it was hit by the Yellow River disaster, and the area has doubled. Therefore, 4,000 hectares of fertile fields are all at the bottom of the water. Shuangyi, no matter how difficult it is, must be thoroughly managed. However, a mosquito carrying a mountain will be crushed. I hope that all the great benefactors will pity these 200,000 disaster victims and quickly get them out of the water and fire. I cannot express my gratitude enough. I respectfully extend this to Lao and all my colleagues in Shanghai. Sushuang respectfully replies, December 13 of the Guiyou year.)

Continued Hearing of the Talc Counterfeit Case 186

Cao Hongzhang, currently residing at No. 6, Zishou Lane, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei, had a late father, Peisheng, who opened the Guangdong Lao Guangfeng Talc Powder Company in Jiuru Lane, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei in the ninth year of the Republic of China. The business was quite developed. In the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, Xu Chengxun, who was running Tongrenhe Company on Min Guo Road, saw that the business was good, so he also used the Guangfeng brand in the store to sell talc powder, which greatly affected the talc powder business run by Cao Peisheng. In February of last year, Peisheng died of illness. When Hongzhang inherited the business, he applied to the Social Affairs Bureau and forwarded it to the Ministry of Industry for registration, and received the Commercial Character No. 4833 license as proof, to prevent counterfeiting. Xu Chengxun learned that Cao Hongzhang had obtained a license, and also used the Guangdong Lao Guangfeng Talc Powder brand as a trademark to register with the Trademark Bureau and apply for a license. Cao learned about it and intended to sue him, but Xu first detained the talc powder purchased by Cao Hongzhang's customer, Wang Shaoqing, and designated it as counterfeit. Therefore, Cao Hongzhang hired lawyer Ni Jiong to sue Xu in the Second Court of the Special Zone for the crime of trademark counterfeiting. Yesterday, Presiding Judge Sun Peng heard the case in the Second Court. After the plaintiff Cao Hongzhang stated the above situation, the defendant's side, Yan Feiguo, came to court to defend. Because evidence still needs to be investigated, the court ordered a continuation of the hearing on February 15.

The Rapid Progress of the Shen Yi Rubber Band Factory 187

Rubber bands are a necessity for factories, and the annual leakage of funds is very large, especially from Japanese goods. In view of this, Ningbo merchants Mu Zixiang, Liu Qingyun, Mu Mingsan, and Mu Yunwu, who live in Shanghai, have spent several years planning and investigating, and gathered huge sums of money to create the Shen Yi Rubber Band Factory at the end of Huishan Road in this city. The factory is purely Chinese capital, Chinese technicians, and Chinese raw materials (supplied by the Chinese National Canvas Factory). It has already manufactured goods last year. The quality is firm and sturdy, and it has been welcomed by various factories, who have adopted it one after another. Recently, the factory has also taken into account the large-scale sale of enemy goods, so it has been improving the quality of its goods and lowering prices as much as possible, far exceeding imported goods, and can guarantee the use of its products. What is particularly characteristic is that if various factories have any special application for any type of tape with special sizes, lengths, thicknesses, they can accept customized orders and deliver them within 24 hours, and guarantee the application. The price of the order is also very low, which foreign goods cannot match. All national goods factories, since there are national goods rubber bands that can be used, should no longer need foreign goods, which is also a major move to stop the leakage of funds. The factory also welcomes people from all walks of life to visit at any time and can contact Mr. Mu Yunwu.

Combined Interest Table for Government Bonds Issued in the Second Year 189

The principal and interest of the treasury bonds are repaid monthly, and the face value is different each month. The calculation of the combined interest is not only different in method, but also cumbersome. When the market price is lower than the face value, the benefits that the bondholder should get are not only the monthly interest increase, but also the proportional increase in the difference between the face value and the market price. Now, Mr. Zhou has calculated the recognized method into a table in his spare time. Within the range of 20 yuan market price, you can find out the combined interest immediately. It was published last year, and readers found it convenient. This year's twelve large sheets have also been published. The entire set is only sold for one yuan. The Shanghai Bank Trust Department and China Travel Service are selling it on a voluntary basis. The proceeds from this sale will be entirely used for rural hospital expenses.

Letter 195

Dear Editor, After reading the news item in your newspaper's local news column on the 2nd of this month regarding the misuse of the talcum powder brand name, I found that many of the contents were inaccurate. Our company has been promoting Guangfeng talcum powder for over ten years. This talcum powder is produced by Guangdong's Lao Guangfeng Company, which has long applied to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for registration and has its distribution office located on Qiujiang Road in Zhabei. The Social Affairs Bureau has repeatedly verified that the inventory is piled up, so how can it be said that the company name is fictitious? The so-called past event of apologizing in the newspaper last year was done by Wang She Sheng, a former partner of our company. Our company acted out of compassion and took the blame for others. Wang She Sheng published a statement in the newspaper and also wrote a written statement, which has nothing to do with the Guangfeng Talcum Powder Company, which has been in operation for many years. The details reported are inaccurate according to the interview. The two parties are now in court, and the truth will eventually come to light. We are afraid that misinformation will spread and confuse the public, so we are writing to request that you investigate and correct the report. Sincerely, Shen Taiyuan Company, February 4th.

Reading Q&A 196

The Seriousness of Reading

Reading Guidance: New literature is a sharp blade, capable of powerfully piercing the paralyzed hearts of mankind; it is a loud bell, capable of awakening mankind from cruel dreams; it is... of course, the effect of new literature is not just so simple. I am just writing two examples according to what I feel.

However, based on the feeling of just a portion of this, this feeling, permeated into my heart, and after being burned by the flames of my youth, it further recalled the disillusionment of past happiness (reading), causing various sweet, sour, bitter, and spicy tastes in my heart, and increased my faith in new literature and my ambition for creation.

But, I am a person who dropped out of school after graduating from elementary school. With such a naive level of Chinese studies, harboring such great wishes, and at the same time facing the current restrictive situation, although the future can always be freed from, comparing the unknowable results of future efforts with the emptiness of the past and present, truly makes me feel somewhat lost. In the difficult and irregular self-study, vagueness often floats in my mind.

In the past self-study, I only kept reading literary novels, recognizing some unfamiliar words, and sometimes I was even too lazy to look up the words. Places that I could not understand (such as foreign literary allusions that are too profound and humorous) had no one to ask. Just like this, just like this, time flew by, age increased, and what about the results of self-study? Emptiness, vagueness.

Therefore, my future, I hope my future, can have a more regular and faster effect than the past.

However, what regular plan do I have now besides reading literature and recognizing words? What faster plan? Ah! This is not an outburst of malicious dependence, it is really something that my brain, which lacks intelligence and is slow, cannot think of!

Reading Guidance, I can only ask you for practical enlightenment. (Letter from Zhou Yun)

We have received many letters like Mr. Zhou's. Although the content is inevitably somewhat empty, and what they yearn for is only a vague hope, it really leaves us with no way to give a specific answer. However, we still feel that this kind of communication is also very important, because this is precisely a kind of problem that friends who casually (play) with literature are most prone to making. Many friends, because of the bitterness of life or temporarily for the sake of bored feelings, mostly use novels and poems to relieve boredom and dispel worries. Some people even completely hold a recreational attitude, all lacking a kind of research (seriousness). Therefore, most are satisfied with (liking to read without seeking thorough understanding), casually playing with it, just like watching a movie, without trying to understand the essence within this exquisite work of art. Like this, reading again and again, although the number of books increases day by day, they have failed to have a deep understanding of any one school of works, or any one author. What remains in the mind is a layer of hazy impression; and their own emotions cannot come into contact with the lofty emotions of the author, so they cannot receive a response from the heart and obtain a spiritual connection. Only looking at the factual structure of the story is easy to make the spirit dissipate and the interest diminish. Therefore, the result of lacking (research seriousness) is often as tasteless as (beer that has lost its fizz).

After this kind of reading attitude is formed, it is very difficult to change. Generally, young people who are unwilling to endure this kind of bitterness then doubt their own (intelligence), or (brain) is inferior to others, and shout out (emptiness) (vagueness). Pessimistic people think that they can do nothing, so they (just muddle along); more courageous people want to come up with some hope, but what they propose is nothing more than (what regular plan?), like Mr. Zhou. Naturally, we sympathize with this kind of reader very much.

What we hope is that Mr. Zhou and friends who have the same problem will first change their attitude of (reading literature), and further embrace a serious research mind, earnestly treating it as a difficult subject to study.

Generally, people who are truly worthy of admiration cannot know their greatness all at once, but will gradually understand their special qualities. It is the same with literature. Truly worthy of reading, high-level works are not necessarily as sweet as honey, as fragrant as osmanthus, and extremely easy to attract people to read. It may often have some bitter taste, or at first glance, it is actually a dry and tasteless story. Readers who savor these works must not only pay close attention, but also have some preliminary knowledge. Otherwise, it will be truly more difficult to directly experience the content of the work than (threading a thick thread through the eye of a needle).

(Close attention) can be cultivated through learning, but preliminary knowledge is increased through one's own knowledge. Regarding the latter, readers should have considerable knowledge of social sciences to lay the foundation for researching literary theory. At the same time, devote some energy to literary theory. (Theory) is the key to opening the door of works.

Mr. Zhou! Your reading plan, because we do not know your life, cannot make it for you. This is your own business. We can only provide you with some advice for your reference. But we currently hope that you will embrace a serious attitude and then study literary theory. Your writing is quite impressive, and your brain is not slow. According to us, you have quite a literary future, so don't be discouraged and move forward! As for how to learn theory, it also depends on your level and cannot be answered here. Fortunately, this department is currently drafting a book on how to learn literature on your own, which will be published soon. Perhaps that booklet can provide you with some hints. However, before it is published, temporarily introduce Qian Qian Wu's "How to Study Emerging Literature?" for you to consult first.

In the future, we also hope that Mr. Zhou and readers who generally have the same feelings as Mr. Zhou can raise some more specific questions, such as (foreign literary allusions, overly profound meanings, humor), etc. for research. We will do our best to answer them.

Children's Weekly - Spring and Autumn

Learning 197

— Jin Xi

Learning is unclear without asking. Learning and asking, learning more and asking more, that's how you get knowledge.

What to learn? Learn the principles of being a person, dealing with social situations, and handling human affairs. Learn the tricks of science, conquer nature, and utilize resources for the benefit of life. Learn to strive for peace and save China. Learn to take on major responsibilities and be a person beneficial to society.

Ask whom? Ask dad, ask mom, ask teachers, ask classmates, ask books, ask the laboratory. Ask heaven, ask earth, ask every stone and tree, ask every flower and leaf, ask every planet, ask every drop of water. Ask the old farmer who plants the fields, ask the miner who digs the soil, ask the merchant who does business, ask the technician who creates tools, ask the warrior who defends the country. Ask all people, things, and objects.

Learning allows you to know the inevitable phenomena of things. Asking allows you to know the reasons behind things. Only by learning and asking at the same time can you understand everything among the myriad things!

Su Dongpo's Wisdom 198

— Shu

There is a dam on Hangzhou's West Lake called Su Causeway. This dam has a history. Originally, there was a famous literary figure in the Song Dynasty named Su Dongpo. He served as an official in Hangzhou. Before he became an official, there was no Su Causeway on West Lake. However, a huge, strange wind often blew down from the mountains on the lake shore, often capsizing the small boats on the lake. When Su Dongpo became an official, he was often worried about this, but he couldn't think of a good solution. But one day, while he was drinking tea, he blew on the tea because it was hot. The single tea stalk floating on the water surface also rose and fell with the waves, but still didn't sink. Su Dongpo suddenly had an idea. He ordered a long dam to be built on the part of the lake where the small boats were being capsized. After that, the situation of boats capsizing indeed disappeared. The dam was then called Su Causeway.

New Tale 199

— Yin Feng

The Man and the Lion

Once a lion and a man were walking together on the road, they were both telling stories about themselves as great. After walking for a while, they gradually approached the stone statue beside the road. When they got closer, they took a careful look, and it was a stone statue of a man and a lion. The man's hand was gripping the lion's throat. The man pointed to the statue and said to the lion:

(There! Look, how much stronger we are than you! We are the masters of the animals.) But the lion quickly replied: (This thing was made by you, so it was made like this: if the lions also knew how to carve stone statues, then you would see a stone statue of a lion stretching out its palm and grabbing the man's neck.)

The Farmer and the Crane

A farmer spread a net in his field to catch the storks that often came to steal grain. Several storks were caught by him, including a crane. This crane was lame and begged the farmer to release it.

(I am not a stork,) it said. (I am a crane. I am a good bird that knows how to take care of my parents. Please look at the color of the feathers on my body. It's not like the color of the feathers on a stork's body.)

But the farmer said: (I don't know whether the color of the feathers is the same or not. I only know that if you are caught with the storks, you can only be executed with the storks.)

This is to teach us not to befriend bad people. If we befriend bad people, we will be in danger of falling into a trap.

Sister Moon 200

— Yin Xu

Sister Moon, whenever it's dark, you wear bright and beautiful clothes, hang in the azure heaven, and smile at us. We play under you, how lively and how proud!

Stars 201

— Yin Xu

Shining, shining, how many stars east, west, north, and south; sky blue, sky blue, countless stars; Big Dipper, Southern Dipper, countless stars to tell; quiet night, quiet night, only see the little stars shining.

Go Ask the Sun 202

— Jin Si Liang

Ming'er suddenly thought of a question: (Why do everyone wear white clothes in summer, but no one wears them in winter?) He couldn't solve it, so he went to ask his uncle.

His uncle said to him: (When it snows and the snow on the ground is about to melt, use a sheet of white paper and a sheet of black paper, put them on the snow, and ask the sun this question. The sun can answer you.)

Ming'er was very surprised when he heard his uncle's words. He thought, the sun is high in the sky, how can I go up and ask him? It doesn't have feet and mouth, and it certainly won't come down to tell me. I really don't understand my uncle's words.

Although he was very suspicious in his heart, one day, he saw it was snowing and was very happy. After one night, the snow stopped, and the sky cleared up, and the snow on the ground was about to melt. He took out the prepared white paper and black paper and put them on the snow, following his uncle's words. He stood beside them and watched.

He watched for about two hours and understood. He thought, my uncle didn't deceive me; the sun can indeed tell me.

It turned out that after he stood and watched the two pieces of paper for more than two hours, he suddenly discovered that the snow under the black paper melted faster than the snow under the white paper. He thought again, and knew that white things don't absorb heat as well as black things; so in the summer, everyone wears white clothes and white hats so that the heat of the sunlight doesn't shine too intensely on the human body, and the human body can be cooler.

He ran to his uncle happily and said: (Uncle! The sun is really willing to tell people; I understand now.) His uncle smiled at him and said: (Good boy, you are really smart!)

The Progress of Lamps - From Firewood to Electric Lights 203

— He Gong Chao

People in ancient times were very afraid of darkness: when the sun went down and the ground was pitch black, their hearts were filled with panic. Even today, the savages in Africa are more afraid of darkness than anything else. Because at night, all kinds of lurking beasts come out; all kinds of dangers surround them. How happy they are to have light. But no matter how much they fear darkness, darkness will eventually come every day. Later, humans came up with a way to get light: they discovered that burning firewood not only provided warmth, but also light. Later, when they were walking, they took a branch from the firewood pile and held it in their hands to light the path. This was the torch. They also discovered that animal oil could be burned, so they made torches and candles. They also invented oil lamps, which were first made of shells and stones, and later of pottery and copper. The wicks of these lamps were made of rush. There were many styles of oil lamps, including hanging lamps suspended by ropes and upright column lamps. There were also several kinds of utensils for placing candles, such as candle plates, candle picks, candle stands, and candle clusters. Rush lamps were made by soaking rush in oil. In the eighteenth century, the Swiss invented the kerosene lamp, which was a major advancement in lamps. Because it had a glass cover, it could stabilize the light, unlike the old-fashioned oil lamps that flickered. As science developed, the progress of lamps became faster. Gas lamps were invented in 1792. Thomas Edison invented the electric light in 1879. As for gauze lamps, arc lamps, floodlights, and searchlights, they were all invented in modern times. They emit such a large amount of light and shine such a long way, that ancient humans would never have dreamed of it.

Thinking 204

— An Fu

Dear children! When you are at home, at school, on the street: aren't there many strange things that you can see? But I know that after you see these strange things, don't you want to run to your mom or dad and ask them? Children! If so, that's wrong.

We should know that after seeing a strange thing, you shouldn't ask first, you should think first. If you can't think it out, think again: think about whether your mom and dad have told you, whether you have read it in a book. If you really can't think it out, then go ask your mom and dad. After they tell you, you should think again, are they right? If they are wrong, then think again and ask again, that's right!

Because, children! You should know that no matter what you do in the world, if you think about it a little more, it won't be easy to forget. Children! Remember this! Think first, then ask.

The Compassionate Siamese Children 205

— Chu Yu

In Siamese customs, the people believe in the king as if he were a god or Buddha. Therefore, no matter what the status of the person, they must become a monk and convert to Buddhism once. If they have not undergone the ritual of conversion, they will be spurned by society and not recognized as human beings. The ritual of conversion, in addition to chanting scriptures, also requires begging for food every morning. When converting, whether princes and grandsons or the children of noble families, they all practice together with the children of poor people, regardless of wealth or status, completely treated the same, without distinction between high and low. If the poor children knock on gongs and stand at people's doors, then any family will definitely take food and dishes to give to these children. This is because the Siamese people, who believe in Buddhism and have a deep sense of compassion, treat everyone equally, so there are no beggars or thieves in Siam. More than ten years ago, a friend who visited Siam returned and told a strange story. One day, he was playing outside Bangkok when three children suddenly came. He thought they were beggars and gave them some bread and fruit. The children sincerely prayed to the west for a while, thanked him, and left. Later, he heard someone next to him say: they were originally very pitiful orphans, raised by the children of nearby families who pooled their resources. After a month, the Siamese king heard this news and felt very pity. He also took out a sum of money to help the nearby families raise those three children. It is said that all three children are diligent in their studies and are now pillars of Siam. Therefore, Siam, which believes in Buddhism and has cultivated a heart of compassion and love since childhood, can be said to be governed by Buddhism. Their country can be peaceful and free from theft and beggars because their people are rich in charity.

Small Experiences 206

— Jian Fen

Pen Holder Mouth In such a cold winter, when you just pick up a writing brush (or other brushes) to write, do you feel that the (pen holder) is as cold as ice? If we want to put on gloves to hold the (pen holder), then it's not convenient to write. Is there no way to deal with the (pen holder) being cold? No! Just use a (fine velvet thread) (the finer the better) to evenly wrap the part of the (pen holder) that you hold. In this way, the very cold (bamboo pen holder) (or other pen holders) becomes a (velvet pen holder). Later, when you hold the pen, the (pen holder) won't be as cold as it used to be.

(Attached note) In the summer, if your hands sweat, won't it be very slippery to pick up the (pen holder)? You can also use this method; but it's best to change to using (silk thread) to wrap it. Later, when you hold the (pen holder) with sweaty hands, it won't be slippery.

Inkstone Mouth When the weather is very cold, problems arise when grinding ink; because the (inkstone water) is affected by the cold air and will freeze. Now there is a very common method that can prevent the (inkstone water) from freezing; many people know this method, but there are also people who don't know it. Now it is written below for public announcement: that is, first put half a pot of (water), and then add half a pot of (sorghum liquor): | ordinary hotels have it for sale, at this time the (water in the ink pot) will not freeze.

(Attached note) Children: Isn't the (inkstone water) used every day? The (pour liquor) will also be used every day. If you have to buy liquor every day, isn't it a very troublesome and expensive thing? No! You only need to use the bottle that you usually use to hold water to store (liquor); when you use it, pour out a little, and when you don't use it, tighten the (bottle stopper); it won't be troublesome and it won't be expensive.

The Adventures of a Little Mouse 207

— Xing Jian

Little Mouse Longtail had never ventured out to play since he was born. Today, the weather was beautiful, and his mother told him to go out for a trip to broaden his horizons. Soon, he ran back. His mother asked him, "What did you see outside today?" "I saw many, many things I had never seen before," Longtail replied. "When I was coming home, I saw a round-faced, round-eyed old man with a beard, wearing a black and white patchwork fur coat, meowing softly, seeming very friendly. I was just about to run over and play with him when a tall fellow with two legs and a red hat suddenly crowed loudly. I was so scared that I rushed home. That bearded uncle even followed me to the door, meowing for me to come out and play."

His mother said, "The one crowing 'ooh-ooh' is Mr. Rooster, and he is very kind. That friendly-looking bearded uncle is our great enemy, Mr. Cat!"

Our enemies often wear a friendly face, meowing very kindly.

Red Flower 208

— Shi Yusheng

Love is a bright red flower. When it is in full bloom, you feel as if you are lying on a green lawn, on a bright spring morning: the sun warmly bathes you, the wind gently kisses you; flowers smile, insects buzz; dew is sweet, springs are clear: everything is sweet.

But if one day this red flower withers, then your father will not even glance at you, your mother will not even turn her head to you, your brother will fight with you, your sister will scold you, what a state your family will be in? And how painful will your life be?

Children, in your pure hearts, sincerely cherish this beautiful flower; love your home, your society, your country, and even the whole world! Pour your hot blood to irrigate it, and never let it wither!

Owl 209

— Chu Jianping

We know that owls are among the fiercest of birds; but they can only come out in the dark night, dashing about and insulting their kind; if the sun comes out, they hide motionless in their nests. At that time, even a small sparrow can bully them, and they cannot resist. Children! Do you want to know the reason? Let me tell you!

It turns out that owls love to reverse day and night. Since they hatched, they have loved sleeping during the day and going out at night. Over time, their eyes have become ineffective during the day. Dear children! Are you willing to be unable to open your eyes during the day and be bullied by others? If you don't want to, then I advise you to quickly develop the habit of going to bed early and getting up early!

Why Do Moving Pictures Move? 210

— Ren Wei

In the movie theater, Ling'er twisted her mother and asked, "Mom! Why do the figures on the white wall move?" Her mother said, "Good child! You asked a very interesting question; but it can't be explained in just a few words. Let's go home, and I'll explain it to you slowly!"

In the evening, after her mother had finished everything, she took Ling'er's hand and said, "I can now explain the question you asked in the movie theater during the day; but just explaining is not enough, unless there is a practical experiment." She frowned for a moment, then suddenly said as if she had an idea, "I've got it!" As she spoke, she found a round tin biscuit can, drilled a small hole in the center of the bottom, threaded a string through it, ready to hang it in the air. (As in picture one) She also dug several larger holes in the bottom (as in picture two) to allow sufficient light inside. Around the can, she also dug twenty or thirty rectangular slits (as in picture three). These were the split flaps to control the light. Then, she folded the edge of the can's opening inward by about two-thirds (as in picture four) to secure the pictures so they wouldn't fall out. After her mother had prepared the can, she cut out several pieces of paper of the same size, drew pictures of running postures in a continuous motion, and placed them in the folded part under the slits inside the can.

After her mother had prepared everything, she hung the can under the electric light and started to spin it. Strangely enough, when Ling'er looked through the slits, she felt that the pictures inside suddenly moved, almost like the moving pictures in the movie theater just now.

At that time, her mother said to Ling'er, "Because human eyes, when they see something, do not immediately lose the shape of that thing; there is a persistence of at least one-tenth of a second. Therefore, whenever an action has not completely disappeared, another continuous action is constantly added, in the minds of people, it seems to have become a continuous action. The inventor of movies used this principle to continuously rotate a roll of continuously photographed film; and applied a projector to project the images, so the images we see in the movie theater can move freely, just like real people!"

Overview of Education in Zhejiang Province (II) 212

Summary of Minister of Education Inspector Dai Xia's Two Lectures (IV) Regarding Secondary Education: The most developed secondary education in the province is general secondary schools, with a total of eighty-three schools (including thirteen provincial ones). There are only twelve normal schools (including five provincial ones), and another eighteen normal lecture classes that have not yet concluded. There are also only nineteen vocational schools (including two run by Zhejiang University and two provincial ones). Therefore, the provincial education funds are mostly allocated to general secondary schools, accounting for 63% of the total secondary education funds. The remaining 21% goes to vocational education and 16% to normal education. According to the Ministry's standards (stipulating that by the 26th year of the Republic, secondary schools should account for 40%, vocational schools for 35%, and normal schools for 25%), vocational education is still 14% short, normal education is 9% short, and secondary education is 23% over. It is now planned to gradually establish one provincial senior agricultural vocational school, three junior agricultural vocational schools, one senior industrial vocational school, two junior industrial vocational schools, and one commercial vocational school within five years, so that the percentage of funds allocated to vocational education will reach 35% by the 26th year. The same applies to normal education, with plans to establish two provincial normal schools, four rural normal schools, and seven simplified normal departments within five years, so that their funding will reach 25% by the 26th year. As for the general secondary schools in the province, apart from girls' secondary schools, junior high schools are established in the old prefectural city areas and senior high schools in the old Taoist regions. Their establishment is quite uniform and meets the needs. Currently, it is planned to maintain the status quo temporarily, with no further increase or slight reduction in funding, so that it becomes 40% by the 26th year. As for the secondary education funding situation in counties and cities, the funding for general secondary schools also accounts for a particularly large proportion, about 74% of the total. Vocational education funding accounts for about 14%, and normal education funding accounts for about 12%. It is now planned to order five general secondary schools to be converted into junior agricultural schools, and it is also planned that all newly established schools in the future will be run as junior agricultural or junior industrial vocational schools, and normal schools or simplified normal schools will be established at any time, so that they meet the Ministry's standards by the 26th year. Private secondary schools are mostly general schools. It is planned to investigate the existing private secondary schools to see which ones are suitable for setting up vocational schools, or whether the number of equivalent schools in the local area is sufficient to accommodate secondary school students, and whether the equipment and funding of the private secondary schools are relatively sufficient and complete. They will be urged to convert into agricultural or industrial vocational schools. For newly established private secondary schools in the future, they will all be required to open agricultural or industrial vocational schools. Since the implementation of co-education for boys and girls in the province in the 16th year of the Republic, girls have had more opportunities to enroll, and their numbers have greatly increased. Currently, most schools above secondary level accept both boys and girls. In addition, there are thirty-five public and private girls' secondary schools that are set up separately. However, in recent years, the number of female students has been increasing year by year, and there is a great shortage of accommodation. The provincial treasury is in financial straits, and adding more girls' schools is not allowed by the facts. It is now planned to add one provincial girls' secondary school, and take back one county-run girls' simplified normal school to be run by the province. At the same time, the number of female students enrolled in provincial junior high schools will be expanded, and classes will be taught separately. The existing public and private girls' secondary schools will be reorganized or expanded to provide relief. The performance of the provincial secondary schools is generally satisfactory. The results of the examinations, except for one junior high school with relatively poor results, show that the number of graduates is more than 90% of the actual number of attendees. More than half of the senior high school graduates are admitted to schools above junior college level. As for county, city, and joint secondary schools, except for a few, the level has not been improved due to factors such as funding, faculty, and equipment, and the results are poor. There are also not many private secondary schools that are excellent. (To be continued)

Vocational Education Society Researches Career Paths of Teachers in Universities, Middle Schools, and Elementary Schools 221

The China Vocational Education Society has been actively conducting research work in recent months. More than 500 copies of the survey on the career paths of teachers in universities, middle schools, and elementary schools have been obtained. Dr. He Qingru and Mr. Zheng Wenhan have now completed the statistics and research and compiled the results into an article entitled "Personnel Research on Teachers in Universities, Middle Schools, and Elementary Schools," which will be published in the 152nd issue of Education and Vocation published by the society. It provides accurate answers to the training that should be possessed, the remuneration that should be obtained, the age of employment, the method of seeking employment, the family situation, and the club life of teachers engaged in various levels of teaching, and all are supported by statistics. It is a pioneer in adopting a scientific research method for occupational content. Young people with career problems can use it as a basis for selection, and those who are already teaching in schools can also take it as a reference for seeking promotion. The article has been printed as a separate booklet. If you want to request it by mail, please attach a one-cent stamp, and the society will send it immediately.
